French Cabinet Approves Peace Plan for Germany, Advocates Forming a League of Nations Army to Maintain the Alliance, and Restoring the Geneva Protocol

(Paris) The Council of Ministers met at the Presidential Palace at 3 pm today, presided over by President Lebrun, and adjourned at 7:10 pm. Foreign Minister Flandin reported on the diplomatic situation before the meeting of the Thirteen-Nation Committee of the League of Nations Council and the Second Locarno Conference. The Council of Ministers approved the French reply to the German memorandum. The reply is divided into two parts. The first part advocates negotiations with Germany. If the negotiations fail, the signatory countries of the Locarno Treaty should fully implement the draft agreement signed on March 19 and advocate prohibiting Germany from building fortifications in the Rhineland region. Talks between the general staffs of Britain, France, and Belgium should be held immediately. The second part contains a broad European political and economic construction plan that distinguishes between issues directly related to the signatory countries of the Locarno Treaty and general issues related to the League of Nations, and uses a collective security system as its foundation, which will be achieved through a treaty signed by member states of the League of Nations within Europe. (6th Havas Dispatch)

(Paris) According to well-informed sources, the French response to Hitler's counter-proposal contains a peace plan that advocates the organization of a League of Nations army to protect the alliance and monitor its implementation. Each major country should contribute four divisions of mechanized standing troops, and each small country should contribute one division. It is said that another part of the response states that France intends to take countermeasures in view of the irreconcilable nature of the German letter of March 31, but this section will not be written in the response and will be declared by Foreign Minister Flandin at the Locarno Treaty country meeting in Geneva on Wednesday. The new French plan also contains the following matters: The League of Nations should amend the treaty. If it needs unanimous approval, it should abandon this system and change to a two-thirds majority vote; amend the peace treaty by peaceful means; transform the economic system; manage armaments; restore the 1924 Geneva Protocol. The document was passed by the entire League of Nations Council, but became a waste of paper due to the opposition of one vote from Britain. According to the protocol, the League of Nations intends to strengthen sanctions against aggressive warfare and seek a solution when the League of Nations alliance contains ambiguous points. (6th Reuters Dispatch)

(Paris) Although the new French peace plan will be sent to the governments of Britain, Italy, Belgium, and the League of Nations Secretariat today, its detailed contents will not be announced until Wednesday or later at the earliest, because the British government has requested amendments to a part of the plan. (7th National Press Agency Dispatch)

German and French Suggestions to be Submitted to the League of Nations for Discussion and the Convening of a European Peace Conference

(Paris) It is generally predicted that both the German memorandum and the French counter-proposal will be submitted to the Council of the League of Nations for discussion. The date of the Council meeting will likely be after the re-election of the French Chamber of Deputies (the Chamber of Deputies is scheduled for re-election on the 26th of this month, with a second round of voting on the 3rd of next month). At that time, it is possible that a European peace conference will be convened at the beginning of the summer this year. (Havas, 7th)

(Paris) The French government's counter-proposal to the German memorandum will be published within this month after being delivered to the governments of Britain, France, and Italy. This counter-proposal consists of two memoranda. One refutes the reasons given by Germany for abolishing the Locarno Pact. The other is a constructive proposal for the organization of a peace mechanism, containing twenty-five articles in total. Its main point is to divide Europe into several regions, with countries within each region establishing mutual assistance pacts, stipulating a military mutual assistance system, and strictly adhering to and abiding by the constraints. This pact originates from the principle of collective security and is based on the Covenant of the League of Nations. Its declaration within the scope of the League of Nations distinguishes it from ordinary military alliance treaties. (Havas, 7th)

(Paris) Le Journal reports that the French new peace plan's suggestions are very broad, totaling no less than twenty-five articles. Although the detailed content has not yet been made public, there is little doubt that it will elaborate on the necessity of a collective security system. Moreover, the collective security system it advocates will insist on Russia's participation, otherwise it will not be very effective. (Guomin News Agency, 7th)

(Paris) The government's counter-proposal to the German memorandum needs to be discussed with the other signatory countries of the Locarno Pact and the countries of the Little Entente. It will not be made public until tomorrow evening. Foreign Minister Flandin received Romanian Foreign Minister Titulescu at 11:30 this morning to discuss this counter-proposal. (Havas, 7th)

French Cabinet Decides to Keep Discharged Soldiers in Service - A Total of 175,000

(Paris) During the State Council meeting yesterday, a decision was made to keep all soldiers scheduled to be discharged on the 15th of this month in service pending further orders. According to a press release issued by the Ministry of War, many new recruits who should have enlisted several years ago were temporarily exempted from military service. It was not until April 15th of last year that they were conscripted. By the 15th of this month, they will have completed one year of service and should have been discharged. However, most of them will still be kept in service. According to the original French military service term, it was set at twelve months. In June of last year, the government issued an order extending the military service term by six months. (Havas, 7th)

(Paris) After the State Council decided to keep the soldiers who were supposed to be discharged on the 15th of this month in service, responsible officials announced that there are a total of 175,000 such soldiers, accounting for half of the normal peacetime quota. This is because the defense works of the Maginot Line in the east (named after the former Minister of War Maginot who decided on it) are the most modern and must be garrisoned by well-trained soldiers. (Havas, 7th)

British, French, and Belgian General Staffs to Begin Talks Mid-Month; British Representative Goes to Geneva

(London) Foreign Secretary Eden departed today for Geneva to attend the meeting of the Thirteen-Nation Committee to mediate the Italo-Ethiopian War and to attend the meeting of the signatory countries of the Locarno Pact to consider the situation caused by Germany's abandonment of the pact and reoccupation of the Rhineland. Before leaving, he consulted with the High Commissioner of the South African Union and the Australian Representative in London on the attitude Britain should take. Lord Privy Seal Halifax will also go to Geneva later to assist Eden in participating in the Locarno conference. The talks between the general staffs of Britain, France, and Belgium to consider plans for responding to unprovoked aggression against France and Belgium will begin on April 15th. (Reuters, 7th)

(London) Regarding the talks between the general staffs of Britain, France, and Belgium, it was previously reported that they would begin on Wednesday, the 8th of this week. Responsible parties have now denied this, saying that with Easter approaching, political circles generally need to take a holiday. These talks will naturally be held after the holiday. According to inquiries by our agency's reporters, the date for the start of the talks has been set for around the 15th of this month. It is also reported that Britain, France, and Belgium have already drafted a plan for air bombing Germany, which will be implemented if Germany commits aggression. Responsible parties have also explicitly denied this, saying that it is regrettable that such unfounded rumors are circulating in the newspapers. (Havas, 7th)

The Thirteen-Nation Committee to Discuss Peace Today; Fears of No Major Results

(Geneva) The Thirteen-Nation Committee of the Council of the League of Nations is scheduled to hold a meeting at 11:00 AM tomorrow. The authorities of various European countries have decided to attend, including French Foreign Minister Flandin, Romanian Foreign Minister Titulescu, and British Foreign Secretary Eden. Soviet Foreign Minister Litvinov cannot leave the country due to matters of state and will be represented by the Soviet Ambassador to France, Potemkin. Turkish Foreign Minister Rüştü is also unlikely to attend in person and will be represented by the Turkish Envoy to France, Davaz Suad. (Havas, 7th)

(London) Foreign Secretary Eden and the Australian representative Bruce (Chairman of the Council of the League of Nations) departed for Geneva at 2:00 PM today. (Havas, 7th)

(Geneva) It is widely believed that the meeting of the Thirteen-Nation Committee to be convened on Wednesday this week will not have major results. The Thirteen-Nation Committee is currently in a very difficult position. On the one hand, the Italian government insists that it will not be prepared to start peace talks within the League of Nations framework unless the League of Nations cancels sanctions. On the other hand, the British government insists that Italian troops must first cease all military operations in East Africa before direct talks can begin. Therefore, this meeting will be preparatory in nature and is unlikely to contribute to a concrete solution. (Guomin News Agency, 6th)

(Geneva) The Thirteen-Nation Committee of the Council of the League of Nations is scheduled to meet tomorrow to discuss the report to be submitted by the Chairman of the Committee, Madariaga, which is a report on the progress of contacts with representatives of the two parties involved, Italy and Ethiopia. The content will cover two points: 1. Regarding the procedures for peace negotiations, Madariaga exchanged letters with the Italian government, and the Italian government invited him to visit Rome. Whether this should be done will be decided by the Committee. 2. Regarding the issue of the Italian army's use of asphyxiating gas, the Ethiopian government has repeatedly complained to the League of Nations, and foreign public opinion, especially British public opinion, has expressed dissatisfaction. This issue will also be considered by the Committee. (Havas, 7th)

(London) The Thirteen-Nation Committee of the Council of the League of Nations is scheduled to meet in Geneva the day after tomorrow to discuss the issue of peace between Italy and Ethiopia. It is widely rumored here that the peace terms to be proposed by Italian Prime Minister Mussolini will be based on the treaty concluded between Italy and Ethiopia in 1895 to resolve the current dispute. According to this treaty, which was concluded one year before the former Ethiopian Emperor Menelik decisively defeated the Italian army at the Battle of Adwa, the entire Ethiopian regime, including its foreign policy, would be controlled by Italy. Political figures here have stated that if the Italian Prime Minister puts forward this proposal, it will inevitably intensify anti-Italian sentiment in Britain. It is expected that Foreign Secretary Eden will request the Council of the League of Nations to tighten sanctions against Italy after he arrives in Geneva. (Havas, 6th)

(Paris) Madame Tabouis, the diplomatic correspondent of L'Œuvre, recently commented on Italy's peace plan for Ethiopia. According to her, the main points of this plan are three: 1. The areas currently occupied by the Italian army should be ceded to Italy as colonies. 2. The Ethiopian mainland, that is, the purely Amhara region, should become a mandated territory, with sovereignty still belonging to the Ethiopian Emperor, but an Italian Governor-General and several experts should be stationed in the Ethiopian capital to handle economic, financial, and international issues. 3. The remaining parts of Ethiopia should be placed under Italian protection, as France does with Morocco. Italy should supervise all matters related to Ethiopian currency, roads, schools, and hospitals, but the rights and interests enjoyed by other countries should still be respected. (Havas, 7th)

German Representative to Leave England for Home Tomorrow

(London) The German representative, Ribbentrop, has been staying here for a week since he arrived on the 31st of last month to present the German government's memorandum on the draft Locarno Agreement. It is now heard that he is scheduled to leave here for Germany on Thursday (the 9th) of this week. (Havas, 7th)

Italian Representative to (Geneva) Attends Locarno Conference; Does Not Attend Thirteen-Nation Committee Meeting. The Italian delegation to the League of Nations, led by Sir Aloisi, departed for Geneva this afternoon to participate in the conference of signatory countries of the Locarno Pact, which is scheduled to be convened on Thursday the 5th, to discuss the new peace plan proposed by the French government. According to responsible authorities, the delegation will not participate in the talks of the Thirteen-Nation Committee because the Chairman of the Committee, the Spanish representative Madariaga, has not accepted the Italian government's invitation to go to Rome to discuss the preliminary negotiations on the Italo-Ethiopian dispute. (Guomin News Agency, 7th)

(Rome) A foreign ministry spokesman stated today that Italy will send a representative to the Locarno conference to be held in Geneva on Thursday, but will adopt a completely reserved attitude towards various European issues until the League of Nations cancels sanctions against Italy. (Guomin News Agency, 6th)

(Rome) The Thirteen-Nation Committee of the Council of the League of Nations is scheduled to meet in Geneva on the 8th of this month. The government has appointed Aloisi, the chief of staff of the Prime Minister's office, Roccu, the director of the League of Nations affairs department of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and Bellasi, an official of the foreign ministry, as Italian representatives to attend the Committee. Political figures previously believed that the Chairman of the Committee, Madariaga, would always come here before the meeting to contact Prime Minister Mussolini on all matters. Unexpectedly, the Committee convened the meeting without waiting for Madariaga to come here, which is quite surprising. At this moment, peace between Italy and Ethiopia must be achieved through direct negotiations between the two parties. If a peace proposal is established after negotiations between the two countries and is accepted by the League of Nations, Italy will not oppose it. However, if all peace negotiations are initiated or even controlled by the League of Nations, Italy cannot trust it. It is generally believed that the convening of the meeting of the Thirteen-Nation Committee is clear evidence of the renewed activity of countries advocating sanctions. However, since the Italian army has repeatedly won victories in the northern route of Ethiopia, the outcome of the battle has been determined and cannot be affected by sanctions. (Havas, 6th)

British and French Ambassadors Hold Talks with Italy; Italy Guarantees Not to Bomb Addis Ababa

(London) The British Ambassador to Rome, Drummond, has received a guarantee from the Italian government that Italian planes will no longer bomb Addis Ababa and undefended towns in Dire Dawa. (Reuters, 7th)

(Paris) The Rome correspondent of the Matin newspaper recently submitted a report on talks between British Ambassador to Italy, Sir Drummond and the Italian Undersecretary of State for Foreign Affairs, Suvich, saying, "British public opinion has reacted to the recent developments in the Italo-Ethiopian War, especially to the Italian army's use of asphyxiating gas. The British government has instructed Sir Drummond to inform Suvich of the information obtained in London and to tell him that such actions can be exploited and exaggerated. With the meeting of the Thirteen-Nation Committee of the Council of the League of Nations imminent, Italy should avoid them. It is reported that Suvich did not pay much attention to this notice and replied that the Ethiopian army had repeatedly used brutal means against the Italian army, so the Italian army used poisonous gas in retaliation." (Havas, 7th)

(Rome) Foreign Secretary Suvich recently met with French Ambassador Chambrun and British Ambassador Sir Drummond to discuss matters related to the meeting of the Thirteen-Nation Committee of the Council of the League of Nations. (Havas, 6th)

Germany and Lithuania Abandon Suspicion and Repair Relations; Economic Relations Return to Normal

(Berlin) There has been resentment between Germany and Lithuania due to the Memel autonomous region issue. Recently, the countries want to restore normal relations. Lithuania sent a delegation to this city on the 9th of last month to negotiate with the German authorities. It has now been learned that both parties have reached an understanding on several important issues, namely the restoration of normal economic relations. More than Four Hundred Dead in US Southern Storm Disaster; More Than Seventeen Hundred Injured

(Washington) The local Red Cross received reports that 429 bodies have been recovered in the southern states storm disaster and the number of deaths is estimated to be over 500. A total of 1,727 people were injured. It is not known how much the material losses are. (Reuters, 7th)

Memphis, USA. A hurricane occurred in the southern states yesterday. According to a survey by the Associated Press reporter, 230 people have died, 1,000 were injured, and the total loss is estimated at $10 million. (Guomin News Agency, 6th)

A major storm has struck the five southern states of Mississippi, Georgia, Tennessee, Arkansas, and Alabama. As of this moment, the number of deaths has reached hundreds and the amount of material loss has reached $6 million. In the central area of Gainesville, Georgia, most of the houses have been blown down and followed by floods. 139 bodies have been recovered from the rubble. Near this city, the number of deaths has exceeded 300. (Havas, 6th)

Atlanta, Georgia. A major storm passed through Gainesville, Georgia today, killing 100 people. According to witnesses, when the wind came, it was like thousands of locomotives being driven together. The extent of the loss is still being investigated, but it will probably not be small. (Reuters, 6th)

US Government New Tax Bill Completed by House Committee; Strong Opposition from Business Community

(Washington) Dalton, the chairman of the House Ways and Means Committee, announced that the committee's review of the government's new tax bill will probably be completed today and hopes to submit it to the House for discussion within a week. Although the Republican opposition is very strong, he is confident that it can be passed in the way the committee has drafted it. Today, according to reliable sources, the business community is prepared to oppose the bill with all its strength when the Senate Finance Committee reviews it. Therefore, even if the bill can be passed by the House, the opposition still hopes that the Senate will veto it. (Guomin News Agency, 6th)

Hauptmann's Corpse Cremated

(New York) Bruno Hauptmann, the main culprit in the Lindbergh kidnapping case, was executed last Friday. His body was cremated here today. According to New Jersey law, the dead prisoners cannot be given a funeral. Therefore, only three or five people, including his defense lawyer and pastor, participated. Outside the crematorium, there were many onlookers wanting to break in, so 28 policemen maintained order at the door. (Guomin News Agency, 6th)

US Secretary of War Speech Strongly Advocates for Modernizing Military Equipment and Building Airplanes to Rival Other Countries

Chicago. In his speech today at the 19th Anniversary of the US Entry into World War I commemoration, Secretary of War Dern said that the US Army, in terms of its equipment, is still far behind other countries. Most of the US airplanes are obsolete. The old wartime tanks could only travel four miles per hour. We are now building hundreds of new aircraft that are at least comparable to those of other countries, but we have few tanks that can reach a speed of 40 miles per hour. The commemoration of the Great War makes us realize that any war in the world may involve distant countries. (Reuters, 6th)

Iraq and Hejaz Sign Mutual Assistance Treaty; A Step Towards Arab National Amity

Cairo. Iraq and the Saudi Arabian country (i.e., Hejaz) signed a treaty of mutual assistance in the event of war or revolution. The text was published today. The people here are very excited and regard this as a step towards Arab national amity. In the treaty, the two countries declared that they would not take any actions that would harm the other party. If there are any disputes, they will be resolved by peaceful means. One of the most important clauses is that Saudi Arabian King Ibn Saud accepts the implementation of Article 17 of the Covenant of the League of Nations (regarding the resolution of disputes between the two countries), even though Saudi Arabia is not a member state of the League of Nations. (Reuters, 7th)

Hungarian Prime Minister Dueling with Opposition Leader; Pistols Fired at Each Other, Fortunately All Missed

Budapest. When the Defense Committee held a meeting on Thursday, Prime Minister Gömbös and Dr. Rassay, the leader of the largest opposition party, had a verbal confrontation. Neither showed any weakness, so Gömbös decided to duel with Dr. Rassay today to determine right and wrong. The two men each held a pistol and shot at each other. Fortunately, all the shots missed. They wanted to fire again, but were stopped by the arbiters. (Reuters, 7th)

Budapest, Hungary. Eckhardt, the leader of the opposition Smallholders Party, had a dispute with former Prime Minister Count Bethlen in June of last year. Bethlen said at the time that his accusations of Eckhardt's statements originated from messages passed from Prime Minister Gömbös. Eckhardt immediately sent someone to Gömbös to ask for an explanation. Since then, there has been resentment between Gömbös and Eckhardt. When the Defense Committee of the House of Representatives convened a meeting on Thursday, Prime Minister Gömbös gave a speech that again invaded Eckhardt, who considered this an intentional insult and requested a duel. It has now been learned that the two men dueled with pistols at ten o'clock this morning. Neither was injured, but they did not reconcile. During today's duel, Stranjanszky, the Speaker of the House of Representatives, served as a witness for Prime Minister Gömbös. (Havas, 7th)

General Nanjirō Reports to Military Authorities on Manchurian Military Situation; Does Not Believe Japanese-Russian War Will Occur

(Tokyo) General Nanjirō, the former commander-in-chief of the Kwantung Army, concurrently the Japanese ambassador to "Manchuria" and governor of the Kwantung Leased Territory, returned to Tokyo yesterday after handing over his duties. Today, he reported to the General Staff of the Ministry of the Army on the situation of "Manchukuo" during his tenure. He then met with visitors, saying that he was surprised that Japan is now harboring war panic. The border between "Manchukuo" and Soviet Russia, except for the Amur River and Ussuri River areas, is mostly unclear, so border conflicts are inevitable. However, it will not affect the general situation between Russia, "Manchuria," and Japan. (Reuters, 7th)

Three Chinese Crew Members of SS Zitemps Brutally Murdered

Singapore. When the SS Zitemps arrived at port today, it was discovered that three Chinese crew members had been murdered at sea with triangular files. US Silver Production Statistics

(Washington) The Metal Statistics Bureau reported today that silver produced in the United States in January was 5,177,000 ounces and in February was 5,313,000 ounces. Mexico produced 6,862,000 ounces in January, but the amount in February is unknown. (Guomin News Agency, 6th)

Austrian Conscription System: Small Entente Countries Unite in Protest, Citing Violation of Military Clauses of the Treaty of Saint-Germain; Reserve Right to Take Appropriate Measures to Protect Interests

(Vienna) The Small Entente countries, namely Romania, Yugoslavia, and Czechoslovakia, due to the Austrian government's decision to restore conscription, have today sent a note verbale via their respective ministers to Vienna to Austrian Foreign Minister Waltinigg, strongly opposing this move, considering it a violation of the military provisions of the Treaty of Saint-Germain, and reserving the right to announce plans to protect the interests of the three countries at a slightly later date. According to Austrian official circles, the Austrian government does not wish to react negatively to this protest, viewing it as a warning to Hungary and Bulgaria not to follow Austria's example. (Reuters dispatch, 7th)

(Vienna) The governments of the three Small Entente countries (Czechoslovakia, Yugoslavia, Romania) have jointly submitted a letter of protest regarding the compulsory labor and military service system adopted by Austria, stating that after Germany abolished the military clauses of the Treaty of Versailles and restored conscription in March of last year, the Council of the League of Nations passed a resolution on April 17th condemning unilateral violations of the treaty. Austria's restoration of the conscription system constitutes a unilateral act in violation of the Treaty of Saint-Germain, and the Small Entente countries naturally reserve the right to take appropriate measures to protect their own interests. (Havas dispatch, 6th)

(Vienna) Following the protest by the Small Entente countries regarding Austria's labor and military service system, semi-official sources here have commented that this was initiated by Yugoslavia and Romania, with the Czech government taking a more moderate stance. The Neue Freie Presse stated, "Austria has suffered more from peace than any other country in the world. There is no reason for the protest of the Small Entente countries. People often speak of Austria's rights as an independent country, but on the other hand, they do not allow it to restore its military. This kind of argument is clearly contradictory." (Havas dispatch, 7th)

Bucharest, Romania: Following the joint protest by the governments of the Small Entente countries regarding Austria's adoption of the labor and military service system, political figures here have commented that this action by these countries is a firm refusal to set a precedent, so as to prevent Hungary from using it as an excuse to abolish the military clauses of the Treaty of Trianon, and is also the first sign of a concerted effort to safeguard security. (Havas dispatch, 7th)

Belgrade, Yugoslavia: The governments of the Small Entente countries jointly lodged a protest yesterday regarding Austria's adoption of the labor and military service system. The full text has now been disclosed by various newspapers. The Vreme newspaper commented, "Although the language used in this protest is mild, it is extremely clear and resolute. The permanent political conference of the Small Entente countries is scheduled to hold a meeting here on May 6th, at which time it will definitely decide on a common attitude that each country should take regarding this matter." (Havas dispatch, 7th)

British House of Commons Discusses Foreign Policy: Sanctions and Peace Negotiations Proceed in Tandem; Opposition Party Strongly Criticizes

(London) Prime Minister Baldwin, due to the government's failure on the issue of equal pay for male and female civil servants on Wednesday, today moved in the House of Commons, asking the House to vote to express whether it has confidence in the government. The motion was subsequently passed by 361 votes to 145.

Opposition leader Attlee was the first to attack the government's foreign policy, particularly criticizing its handling of the Italo-Ethiopian dispute, saying that the government leaders had failed to perform their duties in recent years, causing the impetus to shift from Western democracy to the hands of dictators, and the dangers of war are spreading daily. Since the Hoare-Laval Pact for Italo-Ethiopian reconciliation was exposed, the government itself has lacked credibility. The Italo-Ethiopian war is not a question of whether Italian Prime Minister Mussolini will overthrow the Emperor of Ethiopia, but of whether an aggressor nation will overthrow the League of Nations. Hitler's destruction of the Locarno Treaty and his advance into the Rhineland were the result of the League of Nations' failure. If the Locarno Treaty were to be used to resist aggression, its basis would be too narrow. The entire strength of the League of Nations should be used to maintain law and order.

Liberal Party leader Sinclair and Conservative Party member Churchill both supported Attlee's remarks. Sinclair criticized the government's policy toward the Italo-Ethiopian war, advocating for stronger assistance to the victims of aggression. Churchill believed that the government's policy had achieved nothing, alienated Italy, encouraged Germany to commit illegal acts, and did nothing to help Ethiopia or enhance the prestige of the League of Nations. The lesson from this tragic history is that if the government does not have the sincerity and the willingness to intervene to the necessary extent, it should not intervene in such events.

Foreign Secretary Eden replied that since both sides had accepted mediation, the Italian government had intensified its aggressive acts. From the perspective of the British government, empty mediation in Geneva while the war was still ongoing was intolerable. Now, there must be genuine mediation that can end the war within a limited time frame. The Committee of Eighteen must continue its work. As for the British government's position, it has remained unchanged. The British government is prepared to participate in economic and financial sanctions plans, but other countries must implement them with the same spirit.

Eden went on to mention the meeting planned by the signatories of the Locarno Treaty, namely Britain, France, Italy, and Belgium, saying that the British government could not participate in such a meeting while acknowledging the hopelessness of mediation, but felt that exchanging opinions might not be without benefit. He agreed that the League of Nations should discuss it first, as Hitler's proposal involved countries outside the Western powers. Therefore, this proposal should be adjusted by the League of Nations. If, by the end of the summer, we can see that all European countries are members of the League of Nations, that a new structure for Western Europe can replace the Locarno Treaty, and that security elsewhere is also stabilized due to the League of Nations' direct supervision, then the security we obtain for Europe will be significant. Only then can we proceed with larger plans concerning the economy and armaments. (Reuters dispatch, 6th)

(London) Next, Churchill, leader of the Conservative Party's extreme wing, rose to speak, first stating that the relationship between the government and the majority party was no longer as close as before, and then attacking Prime Minister Baldwin and the Cabinet, criticizing them for failing to prevent aggressor nations from holding a winning hand, saying, "From now on, the rewards obtained by aggressor nations will be far more advantageous than those granted by the Laval-Hoare plan." Churchill went on to discuss the impact of the Italo-Ethiopian dispute on the European situation, saying, "Our country has exerted pressure on France to take action against Italy, but unfortunately, this action has not been sufficient to help Ethiopia, merely alienating Italy and France, and allowing Hitler to seize the opportunity to tear up treaties and advance into the Rhineland area." Discussing Germany's demand for equal rights to colonies, he said that the Cabinet must clearly state its position, "At this moment, the abuse of ethnic minorities within Germany is constantly occurring, so the idea of handing over mandated territories and colonies to Germany cannot become a question. (Members of the House cheered in approval). In any case, mandated territories and colonies cannot be handed over to Germany. They can only be handed over to the League of Nations, as only the League of Nations has the right to decide the future fate of these places. Regarding this matter, the government must hold firm to its purpose and announce it clearly." At this point, Churchill discussed Germany's dispatch of troops to the Rhineland, saying that there was no doubt that Germany would quickly build strong defensive fortifications in the area facing France. However, what kind of consequences would this have on the diplomatic situation and strategy? In his observation, after Germany completed its defensive fortifications on the French border, it would only need to station a small number of troops on the banks of the Rhine, which would be sufficient. Its main army could then leisurely point north and advance to spy on Belgium and the Netherlands. This is a matter of great concern. At this moment, the general staffs of Britain, France, and Belgium are about to hold talks. The significance of this is that Britain has already established contact with France and Belgium, and if the two countries are invaded without provocation, Britain will certainly fulfill its promise of mutual assistance, even if it leads to war. (A small number of members cheered) (Havas dispatch, 6th)

(London) Chancellor of the Exchequer Chamberlain, in the House of Commons today, answered Churchill's question regarding Germany's demand for the return of its colonies, saying that even if Germany had this demand, Britain would not give up any of its existing territories or mandates. As far as he knew, no one had ever suggested that Britain should give up any part of its territory. Britain could never accept such a demand. When the mandate was granted, there was no thought that the mandate could be changed. He believed that the transfer of the mandate required at least the consent of the mandated country and the Council of the League of Nations. The statement by Colonial Secretary Thomas that the British government had not considered and did not wish to consider the return of any territory or mandate had made the British government's position completely clear. Although he did not guarantee the future government, he felt that regardless of the fate of mandated territories owned by other countries, no British government would ever discuss the issue of transferring its own mandated territories. The government recognized that it had a real obligation to the people of the lands it had been mandated to govern. Unless it was certain that the interests of all the people within that land were fully guaranteed, the government would not consider handing over that land to another country, even for the sake of achieving a complete peaceful resolution. (Reuters dispatch, 7th)

Prime Minister Baldwin, when presenting his motion today, briefly stated that the motion for equal pay for civil servants, regardless of gender, was proposed by Labour Party MP Wilkinson and passed by the House of Commons on April 1st by a vote of 156 to 148. This motion was not without merit, but the timing was not yet ripe. There was a feeling spreading throughout the country that the large number of unemployed men was due to women taking their jobs. He estimated that the equal pay motion would increase annual expenditure by £3 million. He believed that Ms. Wilkinson's proposal would not increase the convenience of employing women but would instead hinder it. (Reuters dispatch, 6th)

(London) The House of Commons debated the "Female Civil Servants Salary Bill" last night and immediately held a vote. The majority obtained by the Cabinet was only 216 votes, which was less than the usual 250 votes or so, and had already decreased. Although this case was not related to foreign policy, opposition members deliberately involved foreign policy issues and gave this debate first-class importance. At that time, members on both the left and right sides of the House launched fierce attacks on the Cabinet's current foreign policy. All observers believed that this was beyond the Cabinet's expectations. For example, Conservative Party extreme right-wing member, former First Sea Lord Churchill, held the same tone as Independent Labour Party member Maxton. Even Conservative Party former Foreign Secretary Sir Austen Chamberlain asked for explanations on various key points of the Cabinet's current policy. Foreign Secretary Eden had no choice but to change the pre-arranged procedure and rise to express his views. (According to the pre-arranged procedure, it was originally intended that Chancellor of the Exchequer Chamberlain would conclude the debate). The most noteworthy point of this debate was that the Italo-Ethiopian dispute suddenly became a first-class issue again. The atmosphere in the House yesterday was unusually tense, which was different from the situation during the discussions at the beginning of this year. Recently, news of the continuous defeats of the Ethiopian Northern Army had reached this place, and the House was therefore fierce. Opposition members believed that the defeat of the Ethiopian army was due to the British government's sanctions policy being too weak. Among the government members, since the former Foreign Secretary Hoare resigned due to the failure of the Italo-Ethiopian peace plan, there had been some doubts about the foreign policy implemented by the Cabinet, and these doubts have now been aggravated. (Havas dispatch, 7th)

British Imperial Poet Rudyard Kipling's Estate: £155,000

(London) The estate of the late famous writer and poet Rudyard Kipling is worth a total of £155,000. Kipling ordered that the proceeds from his writings be accumulated for 21 years after his death and added to his assets. His wife, daughter, and son-in-law received the most. (Reuters dispatch, 7th)

Spanish President Considers Issue of Advancement and Retreat

Madrid: The Spanish Parliament is scheduled to resolve the issue of President Zamora's re-election tomorrow. It is expected that Parliament will approve the President's dissolution of the previous Parliament. As a result of the election, the left wing won and the right wing failed, which shows that the failure to dissolve the previous Parliament was not enough to represent public opinion. However, if Parliament does not approve of this matter, then Zamora will automatically resign and be replaced by Speaker Barrio. Judging from the current situation, the Socialist Party has decided to file an impeachment motion against the President to overthrow him. According to Article 88 of the Constitution, if it can obtain the support of three-fifths or 163 of the members of Parliament, it can be established. However, it is questionable whether the Socialist Party can rally this number in Parliament. However, it is heard that the President's side is now considering the issue of resigning before Parliament initiates such a move. (Guomin News Agency dispatch, 6th)

Japan Discovers Large Quantities of Communist Propaganda

Steadily entering via U.S. Ports

San Francisco: According to news from Japanese newspapers here, communist propaganda materials are constantly entering Japan via U.S. ports. Japan is now dispatching police officers to the United States and Honolulu to investigate their source. Those who smuggle communist pamphlets into Japan are mostly merchant sailors who pass through U.S. ports. It is heard that these pamphlets are printed in Japanese by the Communist Party of the Pacific Coast of the United States, and those who distribute them are ship workers traveling between U.S. and Japanese ports. Although Japanese customs and police have been conducting strict searches, large quantities of communist texts have appeared in places such as Tokyo, Kobe, Yokohama, and Osaka. The Japanese police have decided to trace their source and have dispatched personnel to the United States. These people are ordered to cooperate closely with the personnel of the Japanese consulates and local authorities, because these propaganda books are printed in Japanese, and the American police do not understand Japanese, so it is difficult to discern their nature. (Reuters dispatch, 7th)

It is heard that most of these acts of violence are committed by foreign sailors. International Commercial Telegram

Reuters Special Business Dispatch, April 7th

Gold and Silver

London Gold Price: Stable today, up one penny at 140 shillings 8 and a half pence.

London Silver Market: Spot and futures both up 0.0625 this morning, reaching 19 pence 9375. India and speculators bought, China sold.

Japanese Plan New Railroad Network in Northern Manchuria: Increase Number of Trains, Develop Military Mission

Harbin Dispatch: Since purchasing the Chinese Eastern Railway, the Japanese puppet regime has established a puppet railway bureau in Harbin as the center of the railway network in northern Manchuria. Important officials are all Japanese. They are actively building branch lines and adding train schedules to exert the greatest possible mission in military transportation and complete their plans. However, they claim on the surface that these measures are due to the progress of trade in northern Manchuria, the convergence of goods, and the sharp increase in passengers, and are due to the needs of the times. This railway plan is said to be a network for the transport of northern Manchurian industries, and the recent transport volume has increased by 50% compared to before. Passenger trains on the Binzhou Line and the Binsui Line, etc., are very crowded, and the transportation of goods is also overwhelmed. The Japanese are now formulating new plans to implement new transportation in northern Manchuria, which will be completed recently. It is found that the new transportation network secretly contains an extremely large and powerful tool in military terms. Its current train schedule: "Jing"-Bin Line: In addition to the original four round trips between the puppet Changchun and Harbin, it is planned to add two more trips. Binzhou Line: In addition to one round trip per day between Harbin and Manchuria and one mixed round trip per day between Harbin and Ang'angxi, each will be increased by one trip. Binsui Line: In addition to one round trip per day between Harbin and Suifenhe and one mixed round trip per day between Harbin and Yimianpo, each will also be increased by three trips. Not only has it been fully decided, but it is also planned to carry out a mixed train round trip between Hengdaohezi and Mudanjiang, a temporary mixed train round trip between Yimianpo and Hengdaohezi, and two additional trips between Yimianpo and Mudanjiang.

Suggestions from the Shantou Overseas Chinese Mutual Aid Society: Protect Overseas Chinese Going Abroad, Strictly Ban Shipping Companies and Inns

Shantou Correspondence: People from Chaozhou and Meizhou rely on going abroad for work to make a living. However, last month, some who went to Siam (Thailand) were, in the Bangkok area of Siam, accused by the local government of entering the country illegally. More than 600 people were detained, sentenced to 100 days of hard labor, and then deported back to Shantou. Similar incidents have also occurred in Singapore, Annam (Vietnam), the Dutch East Indies, and other places. Therefore, on March 27, the Pacific shipping vessel returned to Shantou from Saigon, carrying more than 400 people who had been expelled. Among them, more than 130 were from Guangzhou and Zhaoqing. It is said that they had sold their property or borrowed money from relatives and friends in their hometowns to get dozens of dollars for travel expenses, and were transported to Singapore for work. This group of over 100 people traveled on a small ship, passed through Hainan, and sailed south. When sailing near a small island in Annam, they ran out of water and food and encountered a large storm. The customs patrol ship intercepted them, and after inquiring about the reason, learned that they were Chinese laborers sneaking into the country. Fearing danger along the way, they were transferred to the Pacific steamer and transported back to Shantou along with those expelled from Siam and Annam. After landing, everyone expressed great disappointment, because they had suffered hardships, which goes without saying, and they had lost their travel expenses. Returning to their hometowns, it would be difficult to make a living. The Shantou Charity Hall then tried to send them to Hong Kong so that they could return to their original homes. After the news of the more than 600 people detained in Siam spread to Chaozhou and Shantou, their families came to Shantou to inquire about the inns and headmen who handled the matter. Those involved in the case had already fled. The Shantou Overseas Chinese Mutual Aid Society specially reported the truth of the case to the government and requested the authorities to seriously ban it in the future. The original text is excerpted as follows:

After the Singapore government restricted the import of Chinese laborers, the Nanki and Bonin companies, which are agents of foreign ships in the city, used the excuse of high exchange rates to increase the third-class ticket price from more than 20 yuan to more than 90 yuan. Due to the restriction on the number of tickets, they privately set up second-tier inns. Because demand exceeded supply, they were able to manipulate ticket prices, which then rose to more than 100 yuan per ticket. Generally, young people were unable to raise huge sums of money for travel expenses and could only stay in their homes. Such monopoly profiteering should be banned.

Two years ago, when rubber prices rose, the Singapore government gradually increased the import quota for Chinese laborers, from 1,000 to 4,000 per month. The two companies outwardly said they were reducing prices, but in reality, they were still monopolized and manipulated.

The treacherous merchants, inns, and headmen colluded with each other, went to the countryside to advertise price reductions, solicit passengers, and handle all ticket procedures. They collected ticket money from passengers in advance. When the passengers arrived in Shantou, the inns did not recognize the accounts, which was like colluding to deceive the villagers. This type of case has been seen repeatedly.

The Bonin and Nanki companies, which sell tickets on behalf of foreign firms, still sell tickets for 40 or 50 yuan each for women and elderly passengers going to Singapore and Penang, which are not restricted. The headmen must bring four or five women and elderly passengers to get this price. Otherwise, the price is over 100 yuan per ticket, with all kinds of exploitation.

When each ship leaves Shantou, the two companies must send staff to the ship to check the tickets. According to regulations, children are half price. If the price is slightly higher, they are forced to buy a full-price ticket. If they do not make up the difference, they are expelled from the ship. Why did the Guiyang steamer hide as many as 400 passengers? The Charlotte steamer hid more than 180 people, and the Yamei steamer hid as many as 24 people. The general manager and staff checked the passengers and heard nothing. It is undoubtedly colluding for fraud.

When the ships depart, the city government also sends many inspectors to the ship to check passengers to prevent trafficking. How could they not have discovered that hundreds of people were hidden? There is obviously something else going on.

The passengers on the Guiyang steamer were mostly lured by inns and borrowed money for travel expenses. Now they are being deceived and imprisoned in a foreign country. Their families are starving and worried. The shipping company and inns should be ordered to repay the original amount and compensate for the losses to show fairness.

The main criminals in this case are the people in charge of the shipping companies, the compradors, the inns, the headmen, and the ship's partners who collude to hide passengers, disregard human life, exterminate humanity, insult the national image, and should have their business licenses revoked and be strictly arrested and prosecuted.

The above eight matters are the appeals of the Mutual Aid Society on behalf of the general overseas Chinese. On the 30th, the East District Pacification Headquarters specially convened a conference for this matter. Those present included Chief of Staff Li Yukun, Military Affairs Director Luo Xianxiang, Political Affairs Director Feng Jianhuang, Shantou Mayor Chen Tongchang, and more than 30 representatives from all walks of life. After discussing for three hours, the following measures were decided: The losses of the overseas Chinese passengers imprisoned in Siam will be investigated by the Mutual Aid Society to recover the original amount. If they dare to resist, they will be arrested and prosecuted. In the future, if anyone is found to be acting as a substitute for hiding passengers in the cabin, once discovered, they will be fined ten times the amount. If there are any gangsters who fabricate Singapore residence permits to deceive people into thinking they are old passengers, after the case is cracked, they will be fined 1,000 yuan, with 80% of the fine given as a reward to the informer. (The new passenger tickets to Singapore and Penang should be registered, and the city government should convene relevant groups to discuss appropriate measures.) The customs officers harassing returning overseas Chinese should have their treatment changed by Customs Director Ye Han. The inns charging excessive travel expenses to returning overseas Chinese should have their fees reduced by the Inn Association. It is said that after the Overseas Chinese Affairs Office is established, there is hope that the above resolutions will be implemented. (April 2)

The Four Department Heads of Guangdong Province Inspect Key Political Affairs in Counties and Cities

—Supervise the Improvement of Various Facilities—

Guangzhou Correspondence: The first three-year administration plan of Guangdong Province expired at the end of the 24th year of the Republic. In order to understand the achievements of the past three years and prepare to formulate the second three-year administration plan, the Southwest Political Affairs Committee decided yesterday that March, April, May, and June of this year will be the period for administering and reorganizing the past three years, and ordered the department heads of the provincial government to take turns to inspect the counties and cities within the period, supervise the county and city mayors to earnestly improve the key political affairs of the past, and immediately instructed the Guangdong Provincial Government to implement it. After receiving the instructions, the provincial government ordered the four departments of Civil Affairs, Finance, Construction, and Education, saying, "Now that the Southwest Political Affairs Committee of the National Government has issued instructions, we have investigated the implementation of various local key political affairs planned by the province for three years. Have the county and city mayors been perfunctory and procrastinating in the implementation of government orders? Can the local people actually benefit from it? It is necessary to conduct detailed inspections, reorganizations, and improvements to increase efficiency. It is hereby decided that March, April, May, and June of this year will be the period for administering, reorganizing, and improving the past three years. The provincial government is instructed to instruct each department head to take turns to visit each county and city in person, supervise the county and city mayors to earnestly improve the key political affairs of the past that concern public interests, so as to achieve practical results and eliminate formalism. The progress of the handling shall be reported at any time for the record. This is most important. This order, etc., must be obeyed. In addition to distributing it to each department for compliance, we also order the Guangzhou Municipal Government to comply with the inspection of its subordinate organs, urge them to be earnest in the reforms, and submit a reply. It is hereby ordered to the department head to immediately comply with the handling, and report the progress of the handling at any time as proof of review and transfer."

Miscellaneous Writings on Rural Hubei

—(Special Correspondent Cheng Jun)

(4) Banditry and Local Conditions in Chongyang

Chongyang, formerly known as Xiajuan, belonged to Tongcheng. Later, it was divided into two. It was first named Chongyang in the Song Dynasty. It has an area of approximately 540,000 mu. It is surrounded by mountains, which account for about three-quarters of the total area. Only one-quarter of the land is arable. The east of the county borders Tongshan, the southeast borders Tongshan and Xiushui County in Jiangxi, the south and southwest are also connected to Jiangxi, the west borders Tongcheng and Linxiang County in Hunan, and the northeast borders Xianning. The territory is surrounded by mountains, and only the county seat is flat, hence the name "Heavenly City." Various towns are distributed, including Dashaping, Baini Bridge, Lukou, Zhukou, Chengshi, Xiaoshaping, Xintangling, Caijiadun, Hongjiaqiao, and Shichengwan. The folk customs have always been simple and honest, and the income from farming is sufficient to maintain food and clothing. However, due to the excess production and the proximity to the border area of Hunan and Jiangxi, the Red Bandits often entrenched themselves in the area, which is a major disaster for the locality. The reporter arrived in Chongyang on the 22nd. A curfew was imposed at night, and the market was unusually desolate, which shows the strong atmosphere of bandit suppression. On the 23rd and 24th, the reporter visited various places and investigated nearby villages. After two days of effort, the reporter learned a lot about the banditry and the local situation. First, the banditry: Badou Mountain in the southwest of the county has been occupied by bandits since the sixth year of the Republic of China, and later seized by the Red Bandits. It has not been cleared for nineteen years. The power of the government has also not reached the area for nineteen years. Yaogu Mountain on the western border is jointly managed by Hunan, as well as the large and small Chakeng, the Guibei Mountain in the southeast, and the large and small Donggang, and the Huangpao Mountain in the south, are all bandit dens. In the nineteenth year of the Republic of China, the city fell twice. The first time was in February. No one can tell the exact number of people killed and property lost. The second time the city fell was on June 24 of the same year. Bandit leaders Peng Dehuai and Li Can led more than a thousand followers to attack the southeast gate fiercely. An uprising broke out inside, and beacon fires rose everywhere. The bandits rushed in through the west gate. Team leaders Liao Chuhou and Tian Daqi, and more than forty militiamen were killed in action. The people suffered great losses. At that time, the bandits were going to set fire to destroy the entire city. An old man stood up and reasoned with them. The bandits were subdued and did not do it. Since then, there has not been a day of peace in the county. In recent years, bandit suppression in Jiangxi has been smooth, and Hunan has also launched a large-scale clearing of the countryside. The remaining bandits have all fled to southern Hubei. Chongyang is the first to bear the brunt. The Xu Yan Gang faction of the pseudo-Sixteenth Division is the most brave. After Chen Jicheng, the commander-in-chief of bandit suppression in the border area of Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi, supervised the army and launched a fierce attack, the Xu bandits were finally wiped out last autumn. The remaining bandits disappeared and did not dare to come out and graze. In recent months, the Pingliu bandits have been rampant. The remnants of the Xu bandits have reorganized in Jiangxi, led by pseudo-Division Commander Wei Ping and Fang Buzhou. They fled from Huangjin Cave in Jiangxi to Tianyue Pass, then to Zhajin, Kuyuan, Jiuqu Ridge, Huangpao Mountain, and then to Dayuan Gaotuan, Jintang and other areas. This group of four to five hundred people killed and kidnapped people everywhere. Even if the ransom was paid, nine times out of ten the hostages were torn up. However, the families of those kidnapped still dare not but offer all they have in the hope of survival. Recently, the niece and nephew-in-law of Minister Wang Shijie of the Ministry of Education were kidnapped by bandits and their fate is unknown. Other scattered bandits, in groups of three or five, harass everywhere and are capable of killing and kidnapping people. In addition, there is the Gong Dehai faction, with about 200 people and guns. Gong was originally a notorious bandit, and was recruited by Feng Yuxian, commander of the Thirty-third Division, and compiled into a guerrilla captain. The bandit nature is difficult to tame. He surrendered and rebelled again, namely the famous Xi Xiazi. Recently, the Red Bandits have been rampant. Gong issued a declaration, expressing that he would not cooperate with the Red Bandits and would help to suppress them in his spare time, but he would not surrender to the government army. It is a strange thing for bandits to issue declarations. Currently, the troops stationed in Chongyang include the Third Regiment of the Fortieth Division of Liu Peixu. This division was originally the Independent Thirty-seventh Brigade and was expanded into a division last autumn. It has been stationed in southern Hubei for a long time, and its military discipline is still good. In addition, there is Shu Qinyi, the battalion commander of the Third Battalion of the Fifth Security Regiment, who is also able to cooperate with the army. Scattered small bandits are often wiped out, but the larger factions such as Wei Fang cannot be wiped out in one fell swoop due to the wide defense area. On the 22nd, a certain unit of the Liu Division pursued bandits to Dayuan. The bandits suddenly changed the flag to the Independent Thirty-fifth Brigade of the National Army. The officers and soldiers mistakenly thought it was a friendly army to encircle and suppress them, and were attacked. Two company commanders and many soldiers were injured. After a brave counterattack, the bandits fled. Their cunning can be seen. Chen Jicheng, the commander-in-chief, arrived here from Puqi on the 24th, and immediately coordinated with the Luo Lin Department stationed in Pingliu, Hunan, the Tan Daoyuan Department stationed in Yichun, Jiangxi, the Feng Xingxian Department stationed in Tongshan, the Li Zongjian Department stationed in Puqi, and the Liu Peixu Department stationed in Chongyang to launch a large-scale encirclement and suppression. The reporter wanted to go to the front to inspect the bandit suppression front line, but because the bandits were constantly fleeing, they were strongly discouraged by the people of Chongyang.

According to the resolutions of the joint suppression conference of the three provinces of Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi, it is divided into three stages. The current stage is the clearing of the countryside. After the clearing of the countryside is completed, it will be followed by self-defense and Baojia. At present, the organization of self-defense and Baojia in Chongyang can be said to have taken shape, but it cannot exert its effectiveness. It is roughly the same as Puqi. The strong men's team is composed of 35,966 people, with only 365 guns, and they rarely have the opportunity to receive training, so it is difficult to use them to defend against bandits. In terms of Baojia, the county originally had five district offices. The first district governs six joint Baos, 57 Baos, and 562 Jias. The second district governs nine joint Baos, 65 Baos, and 785 Jias. The third district governs seven joint Baos, 72 Baos, and 777 Jias. The fourth district governs seven joint Baos, 59 Baos, and 611 Jias. The fifth district governs seven joint Baos, 67 Baos, and 718 Jias. A total of 41,814 households, with a total population of 178,657 men and women, are compiled. Now, according to the provincial order, it is divided into three districts, and the district office will be established soon. However, the drawbacks of Baojia are that it is difficult to find the right people for Baojia chiefs. The Baojia chiefs are still honorary positions, with low status and heavy responsibilities. Such as the requisition of husbandmen when the army is mobilized, the requisition of workers during road construction, and the collection of mu donations by the management office, all are asked of the Baojia chiefs. Wherever the Red Bandits pass, the Baojia are afraid that their crimes will be unforgivable. Therefore, those with a little property or knowledge all flee and are unwilling to accept the position. Those who manage to get the position are arrogant and regard themselves as local emperors. The people of one Bao or one Jia are unable to live in peace. Last winter, Division Commander Liu shot and killed one evil Bao chief, which slightly restrained them, but it is difficult to make them effective. (To be continued)

Songjiang

Commissioner Convened Subordinates for Instructions

Wang Gongyu, the administrative inspector of the Songjiang District, led his secretary and others to inspect various agencies in the county government at 8:00 AM yesterday. He returned to the office at noon. At 1:00 PM, he inspected the drills of the soldiers of the Twelfth Security Brigade, commanded by Brigade Commander Zhao Zanchen. He considered the drills to be proficient and praised them. He then went to the auditorium of the stadium, convened the staff of various agencies, and gave instructions, emphasizing three points: 1. Improve the atmosphere, 2. Increase efficiency, 3. Implement vigorously. He said that public officials have a leading position among the residents. Their words and actions are enough to improve the social atmosphere. Work should be tense, so that they can be a model. He said that vigorous implementation is the most important thing to pay attention to, so as to make politics clear. He then convened the heads of various agencies to discuss opinions on political improvement. At 4:00 PM, he inspected the police.

Kunshan

Fire in the Firewood Business in Broad Daylight

Recently, fires have occurred frequently in the county, causing devastation. At around 10:00 AM on the 7th, a fire broke out again in Zhou Peisheng's firewood business in Qianbang, in the city. The fire was fierce, and in a moment, it penetrated the roof. When the firefighters from various districts heard the alarm and rushed to the rescue, the three large rooms in the firewood business had been completely burned, resulting in heavy losses. Fortunately, it was in broad daylight, and no major disaster occurred. However, the neighbors were quite alarmed.

Strictly Supervise Farmers to Burn Rice Roots

The county suffered a heavy loss from the rice stem borer disaster last year. In order to prevent future troubles, County Magistrate Peng Baichuan has strictly supervised the farmers throughout the county to remove the rice roots. The general mobilization has been completed. On the 6th, the county government sent clerk Wang Guanchu, together with the district office, to various villages to urge the farmers to burn all the removed rice roots to prevent future troubles. Violators will be severely punished.

Suzhou

Zhejiang Water Police Request to Arrest Bandits

The detective team of the Second District of the Water Public Security Bureau recently captured seven bandits, including Hang Xiaoniu and Guan Ada, in Shengze Town, Wujiang County, and escorted them to the team headquarters for detailed interrogation. According to Hang Xiaoniu's confession, he had colluded with others to rob a certain family outside the North Gate of Huzhou, obtained stolen goods for use, and still had a pistol hidden in the wilderness outside Changxing County City, Zhejiang. Therefore, detective Yang Baokang was sent to escort the bandit to Changxing, and a pistol was indeed found in the wilderness. The team was brought back for verification, and the Second District of the Zhejiang Water Public Security Bureau specially requested that the seven criminals, including Hang Xiaoniu, be brought back to Zhejiang for interrogation.

Public Security Bureau Captures Stray Dogs

The Public Security Bureau previously implemented the capture of stray dogs in order to rectify the city appearance. Later, because of the so-called Animal Protection Association, it interfered, so it was stopped. More than 800 stray dogs that had been captured were raised in the shelter. Now most of them have escaped. Recently, a new inspection team came to Suzhou to inspect and believed that stray dogs were everywhere in Suzhou and should be banned. Therefore, Director Zhang of the Public Security Bureau decided to continue the capture. It is said that it will start on the 15th of this month, and the captured dogs will be executed by electric shock.

County Government Urges Dongting Landowners to Pay Land Tax

The county government believes that the land tax owed by the East and West Mountains of Dongting is very large and has repeatedly urged for payment. Because the landowners have no money to pay, there has been no effect. Yesterday, it specially issued a vernacular notice, ordering the heads of various villages and towns to pay first, and then ordering the landowners who serve as Baojia chiefs to clear the payment as an initiative for the farmers. The deadline is within April, and a portion must be paid first. Otherwise, the village and town heads who owe the tax will be detained.

Changshu

Mass Schools Mostly Opened

Here, the masses are forced to learn to read, and more than 700 mass schools have been established, with the village and town heads and Baojia chiefs responsible for running them. More than 480 of them have been established, and they all opened on the 6th of this month. With 60 people per school, there should be more than 24,000 people engaged in literacy work. It is expected that the first phase will be completed in four months. This work is carried out at night, so it is easier for civilians to attend. The number of applicants is very enthusiastic.

Wuxi

Urban Land Survey Completed

The urban land survey in this county began last month. The traverse survey has been completed. The Provincial Land Bureau has also transferred more than 20 land survey personnel who were originally working in Wuxian County to Wuxi to set up a group in Nanshi Qiaoxiang to implement household-by-household land survey. At the same time, the Provincial Bureau telegraphed the survey team leader Xue Gansheng to the province to discuss the concurrent handling of the mountainous land survey in this county. It has now begun, starting with the survey of the Xihui Mountains. There are a total of fifty to sixty surveyors. A separate office has been set up in Wanhuitang, Huishan. After the mountain survey is completed, other mountains will be surveyed.

Taicang

Teachers Hold Graduation Exams

The graduating class of the Senior Normal School of the Provincial Taicang Normal School was originally scheduled to take the graduation exam in Suzhou. Later, the exam was ordered to be suspended. The school received a telegram from the Department of Education yesterday, stating that the graduation exam for the graduating class of the Senior Normal School will be held separately at each school from the 8th of this month, and will be completed on the 11th. The chief examiner will be appointed by the Department of Education and will depart on the morning of the 6th. The test questions will be formulated by each school with three cultivation topics, and the chief examiner will select and circle them. The test papers will be sealed and sent to the Department of Education to determine the ranking.

Passengers on Shatou Ferry Died Suddenly

The night ferry sailing between Shatou and Kunshan departed from Kunshan and returned to Shatou on the 5th. Two passengers who were selling piglets were on board. One got off the boat at Zhitang, and the other fell asleep. When the boat arrived in Shatou, it was already dawn. The boatman went forward to call him, but he was lying stiff and breathless. He immediately reported to the district office in charge and reported to the county government for examination. According to the boat owner, when the deceased disembarked in Kunshan, he was still carrying his bedding and there was nothing unusual. However, the two disembarked at the same time and were both pig merchants. One first got off the boat at Zhitang, and there seems to be something to investigate.

Nantong

The Fourth District Party Affairs Office Ends

Zhang Gongren, a special commissioner of the Jiangsu Provincial Party Department, came to Tong to end the Fourth District Instructor's Office. On the 6th, he addressed the send-off ceremony, stating two hopes: 1. The persons in charge of the industrial and commercial circles should strive for improvement, have a broad vision, and must not stick to the same old ways. 2. Nantong is located at the intersection of the river and the sea. The national crisis is serious. Everyone should pay attention to physical education and quickly organize shooting associations.

Disappointed in Love, Sends Live Turtles to Vent Anger

The Criminal Court of the Nantong Court opened a trial on a romantic case on the 6th, presided over by Judge Sheng. Lu Shouren, an elementary school teacher, was disappointed in love with Jiang Xijue, a young girl. Jiang had married Shen Xiqi, a Shanghai businessman. Lu Shouren wrapped two live turtles in oilcloth and sent them to Shen Xiqi by post. Shen saw that the package was labeled as two boxes of perfume powder. When he opened it, they were two turtles. He sued Lu to the court. After verifying that the handwriting was correct, Lu was also detained for concealing an infant.

Jiangyin

Wuqing Highway Begins Survey

The Department of Construction has started construction of the Jiangyin Qingyangzhen to Wujin highway. Because the deadline is very tight, the engineer Shen Xuepei was sent to Cheng to set up an office in the Qing six district office. He has begun surveying work.

Gaoyou

Chief of Jia Robbed and Both Armpits Burned

At about 2:00 AM last night, more than a dozen bandits, each holding a box gun, wooden stick, multiple sharp weapons, and flashlights, broke into the home of Huang Eryin, the chief of the fourth Jia of the third Bao of Zhangzhuangzhen Houjiaxia in the second district of this county. First, they tied Huang tightly to the bed, searched for seven yuan in cash, five thousand copper coins, and multiple pieces of clothing and jewelry. They were still not satisfied. Then, they used reed firewood soaked in kerosene to burn Huang's armpits, forcing him to tell them where he hid the silver. Huang's armpits were burned, and he handed over ten yuan of hidden silver. Later, neighbors found out and rang the gong to gather the crowd. The bandits were afraid of being at a disadvantage and fled to the northeast with the stolen goods. At that time, dozens of villagers arrived, and seeing that the bandits were far away, they dispersed. Huang was severely injured after being burned and is feared to be in danger of life. The total loss is estimated to be about 300 yuan. The district office has been notified and the county government has been requested to arrest the bandits and investigate.

The Tragic Act of Digging Up and Burning a Child's Corpse

Zhu Yin, a resident of Caiyi Street in the North Gate of the city, and his wife are both in their thirties. They have had several children, but none have grown up. Two years ago, they had another son. In August of last year, when he was only a week old, he died suddenly and was buried near the North City. Yesterday (4th) at about 6:00 PM, Zhu suddenly hired someone to bring inflammable materials such as kerosene and firewood, and dug up the child's corpse, setting it on fire. In an instant, flames shot everywhere. The crowd suspected it was a fire alarm and there were many spectators. After an hour, the child's corpse was turned into ashes. According to superstitious people, the child born after this will not die young. This is extremely absurd.

Hangzhou

Procuring Jiangxi Rice to Regulate the Food Supply

The Hangzhou authorities believe that the price of rice in the urban area has soared, and the livelihood of civilians has been greatly affected. In order to regulate the food supply, they have organized a grain investigation team to go to Jiangxi to investigate the rice production situation. They plan to purchase surplus rice from Jiangxi Province to regulate the food supply. However, because the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway is used for transportation, the freight is expensive, costing 90 cents per bag. They have specially requested the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway Bureau to find a way to reduce the freight to benefit the people's food supply. The railway has sent personnel to purchase freight vehicles and has allocated 25,000 yuan to build a warehouse. Zhang Zili, the secretary-general of the council, went to Shanghai on the 7th to meet with Hui Yangfu to ask for instructions on reducing the freight so that it can be implemented.

Ningbo
